海报写作要点[目的、细节凑]

用途: 电影、比赛、文艺演出等活动
组成: 标题、正文、落款
标题: 简洁、新颖(Poster/根据内容定标题)
正文: 写清楚活动举办时间、地点、参加方式、主,办单位等信息。
落款: 主办单位

Welcome to English Club
Have you ever heard English club? Are you interested in English?Do you want to improve your English? Come and join us!
In our club, lots of activities such as English corner and English debating competition will be organized. If you want to show your English talent, our club will be your best choice. You can also make some new friends here! Every year, our club will invite many foreign teachers to communicate with our members. They will introduce a number of interesting things in their countries to broaden your horizens. We believe you will gain happiness in our club.
English Club

启事写作要点

含义: 向公众说明某事或希望公众协办某事
题材: 招募启事、征稿启事、招领启事、寻物启事
特点: 公开性、广泛性、实用性、灵活性
组成:
标题: 由启事的内容决定
正文: 根据启事的内容和要求说明情况落款:启事者、日期

现象阐释型

现象阐释型作文要求考生对某一现象进行解释说明，分析其原因并加以评论。
其基本结构为:描述段——说明段——议论段·
首先描述现象并说明其现状;
然后分析产生该现象的原因或相关因素；
最后提出建议或总结自己的观点。

描述段

开门见山，总述现象：
Nowadays, there exists a social/economic/environmental phenomenon, which has aroused great concern among us.
举例或利用调查内容说明这一现象的具体表现：
According to a survey, __ .
承上启下，引出原因/因素/影响，过渡到下文：
There are a couple of reasons booming this phenomenon/problem.

说明段

列出原因一/因素一/影响一：Firstly / Above all / First of all
列出原因二/因素二/影响二：Secondly / What’s more / Furthermore
列出原因三/因素三/影响三：Besides / Finally
总结以上原因或因素导致的结果或该现象的最终影响：As a result / Therefore

议论段

我对此现象的思考或看法：
As far as I am concerned, …
In my opinion, …
进一步说明自己的看法或陈述理由

​ Cards

1.现代城市持卡的人越来越多 2.原因在于… 3.”我”的看法
Nowadays, holding cards has become a common phenomenon. According to a survey, over 80% of people in big cities hold various kinds of cards issued by banks, restaurants, supermarkets, etc. There are a number of reasons accounting for it.
First of all, it is convenient to consumers by cards. What’s more, it is safer to carry cards than cash.For example, if one/s cards are lost, the owner needn ‘t worry too much because no one else can get money out without knowing the password. In addition, cards can give car holders certain privileges or discount in service. Therefore, holding cards, especially among the youth, becomes fashionable recently.
As for me, cards have bright future. With the development of science and technology, cards will become much safer and easier to use. From the above discussion, it can be safely concluded that more and more people will use cards.

议论文

【对立观点型、解决问题型、谚语警句型、图表画图型、应用写作型】

问题解决型

这类命题通常首先提出一个有待解决的问题，然后要求考生就该问题提出解决方法、途径。
其基本结构为︰描述段——说明段——议论段
第一段:提出问题或阐述某件事情的重要性或意义;
第二段:列举说明处理某事的方式或解决某个问题的途径;
第三段:针对第二段所阐述的方法给予简要的评论，也可提出个人建议或选择，并阐述理由。
此题型的写作重点在How，即解决问题的办法

描述段

引出现象，并指出这种现象的后果：
Nowadays, more and more people are concerned about the problem of…
现在越来越多的人开始关注…的问题
On the one hand, (问题后果一). On the other hand, (问题的后果二).
As a result, we must spare no efforts to take some measures to solve this problem.

说明段

提出解决方法：
There are many steps which can be taken to solve this problem.
First of all, (途径一). In addition, (途径二). What’s more, (途径三)

议论段

总结这样做(第二段提到的方法)的好处
Only in this way can we… 只有这样，我们才能…

对比选择型【现象、正反、】[字不够举例凑]

这类命题要求比较明确，要求考生比较关于某事物或问题的两种观点或两种做法，并表明自己对该事物的态度。
其基本结构为: 议论段——议论段——议论段
第一段: 引出要叙述的主题，论述第一种观点。第二段:论述另一种观点。
第三段: 陈述自己的态度或观点，做出合理的判断。

说明好处

​ In recent years, __ (提出主题). There is no doubt that __ (该主题) has/have many advantages. Above all, __ (好处一/优点一). Besides, __ (好处二/优点二).

说明坏处

​ As every coin has two side, __ (该主题) also has/have some disadvantages. (坏处一/缺点一), In addition ,__ (坏处二/缺点二).

阐述观点

Weighing up the advantages and disadvantages, “我”的观点
For one thing, _ (理由一). What’s more, _ (理由二).. But i is worth __ (需要注意的事项). Therefore_ _ 总结全文.

Reading Selectively Or Extensively?

1.有人认为读书有要选择 2.有人认为应当博览群书 3.我的看法
Should we read selectively or extensively? Everyone has his own view.
Some people think we should read selectively. They argue that it is impossible for us to read all the books. What’s more, there are many bad books that are poisonous to our mind, and we shouldn’t read them.
But others may not agree. They emphasize that today’s society is not what is used to be. If you want to be successful, you must read widely and acquire knowledge in both natural sciences and humanities, if a man knows much in one field but little in others, he may not be of great use to the society.
However, I think we should read extensively first and then dig into subject we are interested in.

利弊评述型

其基本结构为:描述段——议论段——议论月
第一段: 提出要分析和评论的事物或现象。
第二段: 论述利弊两方面的观点。
第三段: 提出建议或设想。

描述段

Nowadays, (某事物/现象) has been widely accepted by people.

议论段

​ No one can deny that __ (该事物/现象的好处). For one thing, __ (好处一). For another, __ (好处二). However, just as every coin has two sides, there are also disadvantages of __ (该事物/现象). For example, __ (弊端一). Moreover, __ (弊端二)

议论段

In my opinion, __ (“我”的建议). Only in this way can we __ (总结全文).

命题类作文

题目包括三种形式:

句子——ls art education necessary?
短语——My best trip
单词——Dream

写作要点:

审清题目，切勿脱离主题。
分段阐述，结构分明。
表达正确的中心思想。

图画类作文

此类作文要求考生根据图画来审题，提炼出文章主题，并围绕该主题进行论述。
其基本结构为:
第一段: 描述图画中的信息及其表达的含义。
第二段: 指出图画的寓意并具体阐述。
第三段: 对这一现象提出建议或发表观点

确定人称。清晰把握作文的人称线条，切不可上下矛盾，混淆不清。
确定时态和语态。弄清所要叙述的内容事实是已然、未然还是正在进行，从而确立主体时态。
看懂图意。正确理解图画的基本事实，并根据每幅画之间的联系，弄清要表达的主题和梗概。
展开想象。仔细观察细节（图画中的人物、事件、地点、环境、时间、动作等)，依据图画细节对画面的内容加以想象、扩充或补充。

图画描述 → 主题 → 观点

Good news mom！I was accepted to the college of your choice.
In this picture, a daughter tells mother a piece of good news that she has been admitted to a university as her mother desires. There is no doubt that the cartoon leaves us such a deep impression that we can not help thinking over a question: What role should parents play in their children’s growth?

​ In my opinion, during the process of a child’s growth, the role of parents is mainly listed as the following two aspects. On one hand, parents should take good care of their children. On the other hand, in children’s personal growth, parents ought to play a role as a person who helps children develop self-dependence. In other words, parents should encourage their sons or daughters to be independent rather than reliant on others.

​ To conclude, in children’s personal growth, parents are responsible to care for their children. However, considering that they will grow up and live their own life in some day, parents should enable their children to acquire the ability to be self-independent.

图表类作文

图表类作文以表格、曲线图、柱状图、条形图或饼状图为题目，有时会搭配英文提纲作为提示。
其基本结构为:
第一段:描述图标中的数据所反映的问题。
第二段:分析这一问题或趋势产生的原因及影响。
第三段:提出解决问题的建议。

​ We can see from the above chart(图标) / table(表格) that the figures shows __ (反映的问题或趋势).

​ For this obvious trend, there are a lot of reasons and the major ones are as follows. __ (分析说明原因一、二、三).

​ From what we have discussed above, we may draw the conclusion that __ (提出结论). Therefore, __ (提出建议或解决办法). Only in this way can we __ (得到更好的结果)

(2022)假设你是光明大学大二学生李华，有英国学生来学校参观，向教务处申请导游的职位，并说明你的优点。
个人优势：
1.了解学校文化;
2.性格;
3.英语口语流利。
注意:
1.100词左右，开头结尾已经给出，不计入总词数;
2.可以适当增加细节，以使行文连贯。

Dear sir,

​ My name is Li Hua, a sophomore form Guangming university. I am writing to apply for the position as a tour guide. There are several factors contributing to my application.
​ First of all, I have a good knowledge of our college’s culture, so can help the British students to learn about our college more quickly. Most importantly, I vam a cheerful and outgoing person so I can easily integrate with others. I believe I will bring an unforgettable trip to these foreign students.
​ I would appreciate it if you could give me this opportunity. Looking forward to you early reply！
​ Yours,
​ Li Hua

议论文[3-4段] [字不够举例凑]

【对立观点型、解决问题型、谚语警句型、图表画图型、应用写作型】

对立观点型

有人认为放鞭炮是好事，为什么？
有人认为放鞭炮是坏事，为什么？
我的看法…
【截图】

There is no denying the fact that setting off firecrackers has been a hotly debated topic in China.

不可否认，燃放鞭炮在中国一直是一个备受争议的话题。

People’s opinions differ sharply on this issue.

在这个问题上，人们的意见大相径庭。

Some hold the positive view.

有些人持积极的观点。

They say that it is an ancient Chinese custom which should be preserved.

他们说这是一种古老的中国习俗，应该保留下来。

Therefore, it is goes without saying that it is of great of importance to practice the proverb ___
因此，不用说，实践这句谚语非常重要

They also claim that firecrackers make festivals and holiday occasions more colorful and entertaining for both adults and children.

他们还声称，鞭炮使节日和节日活动更加丰富多彩，对成人和儿童都更具娱乐性。

Without firecrackers, festivals would become dull and cheerless.

如果没有鞭炮，节日就会变得沉闷乏味。

Others, however, hold the opposite view.

然而，其他人持相反观点。

They maintain that firecrackers should be banned.

他们坚持认为应该禁止燃放鞭炮。

They point out that firecrackers are responsible for fires, which destroy property, and for injuries suffered both by the people who set them off and by innocent bystanders.

他们指出，鞭炮是火灾的罪魁祸首，火灾摧毁了财产，也造成了燃放者和无辜旁观者的受伤。

They also argue that firecrackers are a waste of money and resources.

他们还认为鞭炮是对金钱和资源的浪·费。

Personally, I believe that we should not go to extremes.

就我个人而言，我认为我们不应该走极端。

On the one hand, we should preserve the old custom of letting off firecrackers;

一方面，我们应该保留燃放鞭炮的古老习俗；

on the other hand, we should make it harmless.

另一方面, 我们应该使其无害。

This can be done by banning firecrackers from public places.

这可以通过禁止在公共场所燃放鞭炮来实现。

In addition, the setting off of firecrackers should be restricted to festival days.

此外，燃放鞭炮应限制在节日期间。

解决问题型==【截图】==

目前盗版的现象比较严重
造成这种现象的原因及其危害
我们应该怎么做

万能开头句式

There is no denying the fact that
There is no doubt that,
Nobody can deny the fact that
Nobody could have failed to notice the fact that

My View on Fake Commodities

Nobody could have failed to没有做… notice the fact that fake commodities have been a grave严重的 problem with which we are confronted面对.

没有人会不注意到，假冒商品是我们面临的一个严重问题。

Fake and shoddy goods flood the market.

假冒伪劣商品充斥市场。

Taking a look around, we can find examples too numerous to list:

纵观四周，我们可以发现不胜枚举的例子：

pirated editions of books and files, food and drinks of poor quality and the like.

盗版书籍和文件、劣质食品和饮料等。

A number of factors could account for解释 the problem, but the following might be the most critical ones.

有很多因素可以解释问题，但以下可能是最关键的因素。

In view of the seriousness of this problem. effective measures must be taken before things get worse.

鉴于这个问题的严重性。在情况恶化之前必须采取有效措施。

First and foremost, it is essential that至关重要的是 laws and regulations be worked out and enforced to ban the manufacture and circulation of fake and shoddy goods.

首先，必须制定和执行法律法规，禁止假冒伪劣商品的制造和流通。

Additionally, the public should enhance their awareness of identifying and refusing sub-standard commodities.

此外，公众应提高识别和拒绝不合标准商品的意识。

With proper laws and an alert public, it will only be a matter of time for fake and shoddy goods to become things of the past.

有了适当的法律和警惕的公众，假冒伪劣商品成为过去只是时间问题。

…

Last but not least, Fake and shoddy goods are bound to generate severe consequences if we keep turning a blind eye to them,

最后但最重要的是, 如果我们继续视而不见，假冒伪劣商品势必会产生严重后果，

现状 原因 危害 建议
① 现状+举例

First and foremost
Additionally
Last but not least

经济发展类

A number of factors could account for the change in the chart, but the following are the most critical ones.

许多因素可以解释图表中的变化，但以下是最关键的因素。

First, thanks to the policy of reform and opening-up, the nation’s economy has been developing at a considerably high speed in the past decades.

首先，得益于改革开放政策，过去几十年来，我国经济以相当高的速度发展。

Therefore, people have more extra money to improve their housing.

因此，人们有更多的额外资金来改善他们的住房。

Secondly, other relevant state policies and the boom of real estate industry provide citizens with more opportunities to choose their own dwelling places.

其次，其他相关国家政策和房地产行业的繁荣为公民提供了更多选择自己住所的机会。

Last but not least, people have attached greater importance to their quality of life.

最后但同样重要的是，人们更加重视自己的生活质量。

Thus more of them have purchased houses in their own favor.

因此，他们中更多的人购买了对自己有利的房子。

In a word, this chart is a perfect index of China’s fast expanding economy and people’s rising standard of living.

总之，这张图表是中国快速增长的经济和人民生活水平不断提高的完美指标。

Although a series of problems have arisen in the process, it is reasonable for us to believe that they can be solved in the near future with effective measures taken by both the government and the public.

尽管在这个过程中出现了一系列问题，但我们有理由相信，只要政府和公众采取有效措施，这些问题可以在不久的将来得到解决。

陈述利弊型

There is no denying the fact that setting off firecrackers has been a hotly debated topic in China because there are advantages as well as disadvantages.

The Internet is playing an increasingly important role in people’s life.

But just as a coin has two sides, the Internet has its own drawbacks which should not be neglected.

定题作文

议论文必须要有题目

李华沉迷于电脑游戏中，影响了学习。作为他的好朋友，你打算怎么帮他？

题目： My View on…(英语学习之我见)除了放在中间的介词/冠词,都要大写

My View on Computer Games

列大纲

现象：[例子不胜枚举举个例子：]李华沉迷于电脑游戏中，影响了学习。问题(套话[毫无疑问现在玩游戏是我们不得不面对的问题了])
危害：如果我们对这个现象置若罔闻会造成严重的后果 ① 对眼镜不好 ② 不利于家庭关系 ③ 不利于身体健康 ④ 浪费钱
建议：套话 ① 如果我是他 找爸妈谈谈 ② it is important…体育运动很重要 ③it is time…是时候要干嘛(交朋友) ④1234词 我的建议… ⑤旅游
如果我们将计算机的优势最大化利益最小化我们….
结尾：套话
